[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[39mreturn UINT32_MAX;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:     [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m See file-format.txt section [0m[1;92m2.1.1.2[0m[39m.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:     [0m[39mstatic const uint8_t check_sizes[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mLZMA_CHECK_ID_MAX + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m{[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m,[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m,[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m,[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m,[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m,[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m64[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m64[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:     [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:     [0m[39mreturn check_sizes[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned int[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtype[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:        This document describes the .xz file format [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfilename suffix[0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m336:2[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m1.1[0m[39m.[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Stream Flags[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m337[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m338[0m[39m:        The first byte of Stream Flags is always a null byte. In the[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m339[0m[39m:        future, this byte may be used to indicate a new Stream version[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m340[0m[39m:        or other Stream properties.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m341[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m342[0m[39m:        The second byte of Stream Flags is a bit field:[0m                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m:    [0m[39mcase LZMA_CHECK_TREE:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mcheck->buffer.u32[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;35mconv32le[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcheck->state.tree[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m177[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mbreak;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe evaluation report reveals a **critical heap-use-after-free vulnerability** in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe tree checksum implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`treeck.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. After analyzing the code snippets, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mI've identified the root cause:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Cyclic Graph Structure**: The `create_tree` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m51[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m53[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintentionally creates cycles by adding parent backreferences when `block_size == [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_BLOCK_WIDTH * MAX_BLOCK_HEIGHT`:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   if [0m[1;39m([0m[33mi[0m[39m==node->edge_count-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m && node->[0m[33mblock_size[0m[39m==MAX_BLOCK_WIDTH*MAX_BLOCK_HEIGHT[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       node->edges[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = parent;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Creates cycle: parent → child → parent[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Unsafe Memory Management**: The `compute_tree_checksum` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m66[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m93[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmixes checksum computation with memory deallocation in a single traversal. It frees[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnodes immediately after processing [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m89[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->edges[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   [0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Use-After-Free Scenario**: When a parent node recursively processes its [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mchildren:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parent enters loop to process children [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m79[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Child is processed recursively [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m82[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Child encounters backlink to parent and recursively calls it[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Parent returns [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39malready STATE_VISITED/STATE_HASHED[0m[1;39m)[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Child frees itself [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m89[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[1;39m)[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Control returns to parent's loop which continues accessing freed memory**[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe state machine [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSTATE_CLEAR/VISITED/HASHED[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m prevents infinite loops but doesn't [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent use-after-free because nodes are freed during traversal while still being [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferenced.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Observations[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The tree checksum is an **experimental/non-standard feature** using reserved [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCheck ID [0m[1;36m0x0B[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The codebase pattern in `index_tree_node_end` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindex.[0m[1;92mc:193[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m207[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows the proper [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproach: separate cleanup in post-order traversal[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The tree is temporary and fully created/destroyed within each `[0m[1;35mlzma_tree[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer correctly exposes the bug by crafting input that creates cycles[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Approach: Separate Checksum Computation from Memory Cleanup[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFollowing the existing pattern in `index_tree_node_end`, I will separate the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomputation phase from the cleanup phase. This is the safest approach that:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Handles cycles correctly[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Follows established patterns in the codebase[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Maintains clear separation of concerns[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Requires minimal risk of breaking existing functionality[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Steps[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Modify `compute_tree_checksum` in `src/liblzma/check/treeck.c`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Remove memory deallocation from the computation function:**[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Delete lines [0m[1;36m88[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m90[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode->edges[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and `[0m[1;35mfree[0m[1;39m([0m[39mnode[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` calls[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keep all computation and state management logic intact[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function should only compute checksums, not free memory[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add New `free_tree_node` Function in `src/liblzma/check/treeck.c`[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Insert after `compute_tree_checksum` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbefore `lzma_tree`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCreate a dedicated cleanup function that safely handles cycles:[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use post-order traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfree children before parent[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Track already-freed nodes using a new STATE_FREED state to handle cycles[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Only free edges array and node structure, no computation[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe function should:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Check if node is NULL or already freed [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreturn early[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Iterate through all edges[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. For each child that hasn't been freed, recursively call `free_tree_node`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Mark current node as STATE_FREED to prevent double-free[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Free the edges array[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Free the node itself[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Add STATE_FREED Constant in `src/liblzma/check/treeck.h`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Add after line [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter STATE_HASHED definition[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:**[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Define `STATE_FREED` as value [0m[1;36m3[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This state marks nodes that have been freed, preventing double-free when cycles [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexist[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Update `lzma_tree` in `src/liblzma/check/treeck.c`[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Modify the function at lines [0m[1;36m95[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m102[0m[39m:**[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After line [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mafter `compute_tree_checksum` call[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, add a call to the new [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup function[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The sequence should be:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Create tree[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Compute checksum [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno freeing[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Clean up tree [0m[1;39m([0m[39mseparate traversal[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Return checksum[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSpecifically:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Store the result of `[0m[1;35mcompute_tree_checksum[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot, [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` in a temporary variable[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- XOR it with the checksum parameter[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Call `[0m[1;35mfree_tree_node[0m[1;39m([0m[39mroot[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to clean up the entire tree[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Return the accumulated checksum[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m: Handle Edge Case When Root is NULL[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**In the `lzma_tree` function:**[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add a NULL check after `create_tree` returns[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- If root is NULL, skip both checksum computation and cleanup[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This can happen when input is too small or depth limit is immediately reached[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Justification[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why This Is Optimal:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns**: The `index_tree_node_end` function in `index.c` [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrates the same pattern of post-order cleanup that the xz codebase already [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muses successfully[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Handles Cycles Safely**: By using STATE_FREED to track already-freed nodes, we[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprevent double-free errors when cycles exist[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Preserves Computation Logic**: The checksum computation algorithm remains [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompletely unchanged, ensuring identical results[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Clear Separation**: Computation and cleanup are in separate functions, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimproving maintainability and reducing complexity[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Minimal Risk**: No changes to the tree creation logic or the computation [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malgorithm minimize the risk of introducing new bugs or breaking existing tests[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**How It Addresses the Issue:**[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The use-after-free is eliminated because nodes are not freed until after all [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomputation is complete[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The parent's loop can safely complete because child nodes are not freed during [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtraversal[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory is still fully cleaned up through the dedicated cleanup function[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Cycles are handled correctly through the STATE_FREED tracking[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effects:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Slight Performance Impact**: Two tree traversals instead of one [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcompute then [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcleanup[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: Tree depth is limited to [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m levels [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m99[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so overhead is [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mminimal[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The xz codebase comment in `index.[0m[1;92mc:197[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m198[0m[39m` notes that recursion is [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39macceptable for reasonable tree depths[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Additional Memory During Execution**: Tree remains in memory during entire [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`lzma_tree` call[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mitigation: Already the case - tree must exist until checksum is computed[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No practical difference in peak memory usage[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Similar Solutions in Codebase:**[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `index_tree_node_end` function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindex.[0m[1;92mc:193[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m207[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m demonstrates the exact same [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern:[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Post-order traversal [0m[1;39m([0m[39mchildren before parent[0m[1;39m)[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Recursive cleanup function separate from usage[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Comments acknowledging recursion is fine for reasonable depths[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis validates that the approach is consistent with xz's coding patterns and [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mphilosophy.[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
